configuration, chain creation, and per-request execution.\\n\\n**Filter Definition and Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h):**\\nThe core filter interfaces are defined in envoy/http/filter.h, which includes Filter, StreamFilter, StreamDecoderFilter, StreamEncoderFilter, and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks. These provide the plugin interface for HTTP filters.\\n\\n**Filter Factory and Chain Management (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):**\\nThis file defines the filter factory mechanism with FilterFactoryCb (factory callback function type), FilterContext (contextual information about a filter), FilterChainOptions (options for chain creation), FilterChainManager (interface for applying filter factories), and FilterChainFactory (interface for creating filter chains).\\n\\n**Filter Configuration Factory (envoy/server/filter_config.h):**\\nHttpFilterConfigFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory define the extension point where filter implementations register themselves. Each HTTP filter plugin must implement NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory to be discoverable by Envoy's registry system.\\n\\n**Filter Manager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and filter_manager.cc):**\\nFilterManager is the core orchestrator that implements FilterChainManager. It manages the per-request filter chain execution, maintaining separate decoder and encoder filter chains. The FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl inner class provides the callbacks used during filter chain creation. FilterManager contains the critical per-request filter execution methods: decodeHeaders, decodeData, decodeTrailers for incoming request path and encodeHeaders, encodeData, encodeTrailers for outgoing response path. ActiveStreamFilterBase provides the base implementation for both decoder and encoder filter wrappers.\\n\\n**Filter Chain Creation (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc):**\\nFilterChainUtility provides createFilterChainForFactories to create the actual filter chain from a list of factory callbacks. ConnectionManagerImpl orchestrates HTTP streams and invokes filter chain creation. ConnectionManagerConfig holds the filter factories and provides the FilterChainFactory implementation.\\n\\n**Filter Execution Flow:**\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives: 1) ConnectionManagerImpl::onNewStream is called, 2) FilterManager::createFilterChain creates the filter chain via FilterChainFactory, 3) FilterChainUtility processes each configured filter factory by calling FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb, 4) FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl adds filters to the decoder/encoder chains, 5) FilterManager then executes filters through decodeHeaders/decodeData/decodeTrailers methods in the decoder path and encodeHeaders/encodeData/encodeTrailers in the encoder path, managing iteration state and allowing filters to buffer data or short-circuit the chain.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3050,"cache_read_input_tokens":73610,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3050},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"508d90bd-bfa1-4439-a606-543d39db0e46","uuid":"86d64ada-6214-4dc2-a05f-1a02877e4df8"}

FilterManager contains the critical per-request filter execution methods: decodeHeaders, decodeData, decodeTrailers for incoming request path and encodeHeaders, encodeData, encodeTrailers for outgoing response path. ActiveStreamFilterBase provides the base implementation for both decoder and encoder filter wrappers.\\n\\n**Filter Chain Creation (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc):**\\nFilterChainUtility provides createFilterChainForFactories to create the actual filter chain from a list of factory callbacks. configuration, chain creation, and per-request execution.\\n\\n**Filter Definition and Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h):**\\nThe core filter interfaces are defined in envoy/http/filter.h, which includes Filter, StreamFilter, StreamDecoderFilter, StreamEncoderFilter, and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks. These provide the plugin interface for HTTP filters.\\n\\n**Filter Factory and Chain Management (envoy/http/filter_factory.h):**\\nThis file defines the filter factory mechanism with FilterFactoryCb (factory callback function type), FilterContext (contextual information about a filter), FilterChainOptions (options for chain creation), FilterChainManager (interface for applying filter factories), and FilterChainFactory (interface for creating filter chains).\\n\\n**Filter Configuration Factory (envoy/server/filter_config.h):**\\nHttpFilterConfigFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory define the extension point where filter implementations register themselves. Each HTTP filter plugin must implement NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory to be discoverable by Envoy's registry system.\\n\\n**Filter Manager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and filter_manager.cc):**\\nFilterManager is the core orchestrator that implements FilterChainManager. It manages the per-request filter chain execution, maintaining separate decoder and encoder filter chains. The FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl inner class provides the callbacks used during filter chain creation. FilterManager contains the critical per-request filter execution methods: decodeHeaders, decodeData, decodeTrailers for incoming request path and encodeHeaders, encodeData, encodeTrailers for outgoing response path. ActiveStreamFilterBase provides the base implementation for both decoder and encoder filter wrappers.\\n\\n**Filter Chain Creation (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc):**\\nFilterChainUtility provides createFilterChainForFactories to create the actual filter chain from a list of factory callbacks. FilterChainHelper processes filter configurations and creates FilterChainUtility instances to handle filter instantiation.\\n\\n**Named Filter Factory Callbacks (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h):**\\nNamedHttpFilterFactoryCb struct bundles a filter name with its FilterFactoryCb. HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl implements dynamic discovery of HTTP filter configurations.\\n\\n**HTTP Connection Manager (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h, source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h, source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h):**\\nHttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory creates the HTTP connection manager network filter. ConnectionManagerImpl orchestrates HTTP streams and invokes filter chain creation. ConnectionManagerConfig holds the filter factories and provides the FilterChainFactory implementation.\\n\\n**Filter Execution Flow:**\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives: 1) ConnectionManagerImpl::onNewStream is called, 2) FilterManager::createFilterChain creates the filter chain via FilterChainFactory, 3) FilterChainUtility processes each configured filter factory by calling FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb, 4) FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl adds filters to the decoder/encoder chains, 5) FilterManager then executes filters through decodeHeaders/decodeData/decodeTrailers methods in the decoder path and encodeHeaders/encodeData/encodeTrailers in the encoder path, managing iteration state and allowing filters to buffer data or short-circuit the chain.\"\n}\n","numLines":68,"startLine":1,"totalLines":68}}}
